Earlier in 3.13 — **§51.11.22 added — Slice 122: The Sovereign Cryptographic Key Manager & Dynamic Synthesis.** The Layer-4 ignition infrastructure, zero-hardcoding — and the **root-cause crypto upgrade**: Slice 120's symmetric HMAC let any verifier also forge (the loop could mint its own roadmap), so Layer-4 signing moves to **asymmetric Ed25519** — operator holds the private key, the loop gets only the public key and **cannot forge (mathematical, not policy)**. Private key = `scrypt(passphrase, salt)`, derived live, **never stored** (no plaintext .env, proven the passphrase never hits disk). `roadmap_synthesizer.py` drafts an unsigned, authority-free, conservative `.jarvis/roadmap.draft.yaml`. **Refused the "one-click web sign" button** — the gateway's own invariant forbids a browser endpoint that mints authority; exposed the draft READ-ONLY + kept signing a local passphrase-gated CLI act. 10 tests (round-trip + air-gap: foreign-key roadmap rejected, passphrase never on disk; fail-closed) + Slice 120 regression 21/21; `cryptography` added to requirements. T4 now armable end-to-end. Built the real, defensible thing instead: a parallel cage siege (composes Slice 115 ledger + Slice 84 `run_sweep`) yielding **adversarial-volume** + **concurrency-correctness** statistics that *complement* the T5 clock, never substitute for it. Refused 50 live self-modifying loops (read-only siege only). Solved the "thread-safe ledger" correctly: a hash chain is irreducibly sequential, so we parallelize the expensive cage eval and serialize only the cheap chain-link through one lock-guarded `ThreadSafeLedger` → provably-unbroken chain (proven: 1600 receipts / 16 threads / `verify_ledger` True / contiguous seqs). `MatrixReport` carries an honesty `disclaimer` + emits no calendar-equivalence field; `launch_simulation_matrix.sh --concurrency N`; 7 tests + Slice 115 regression clean (8/8); live smoke 570 attacks/3.51 % escape/chain intact. Operator-driven post-bt-2026-05-26-184355 PURE-DW v15 soak audit ("for my local 16GB M1 Mac, how many agents can O+V deploy or spawn?"). 6 concurrency surfaces enumerated with owner module + line number (BackgroundAgentPool / SubagentScheduler / MAX_PARALLEL_SCOPES / AST helper pool / 18 intake sensors / Aegis daemon); hard memory envelope = `psutil.virtual_memory().total × 0.75` = 12,288 MB on 16 GB M1 (empirically verified from v15 debug.log: cap=12288MB warn=10445MB peak RSS 1927MB); per-component additive memory budgets; recommended concurrency settings by hardware tier (16/32/64/96+ GB) with auto-scaling cap. **Net empirical answer**: ~34 asyncio tasks + subprocesses at max fan-out, ~8-12 doing real work simultaneously, ~12-16% of memory cap used at peak. **Binding constraint is provider cost, NOT local RAM.** No hardcoding (every figure read from psutil + debug.log + source line refs). **Version**: 3.5 (2026-05-12 — **Treefinement L2 first validation soak — wiring SAFETY validated, FUNCTIONALITY exercise gap documented honestly**: First operator-paced Phase 9 validation soak under the v3.4 production wiring. Session `bt-2026-05-12-171129` ran 828s wall-clock with `JARVIS_L2_TREEFINEMENT_ENABLED=true` + `JARVIS_L2_BRANCHING_STRATEGY=bfs` + archive surfaces enabled; clean shutdown via WallClockWatchdog (`stop_reason=wall_clock_cap+atexit_fallback` → `session_outcome=complete` per v2.96 Layer 8 discipline). **What the soak validated** (wiring safety): (1) Boot path with Treefinement env block is safe — no crashes, no tracebacks, no production-wiring-attributed errors; (2) Six-layer stack boots cleanly under tree-mode config — GovernedLoopService + IntakeLayer (16 sensors) + DreamEngine (DW + Claude both active) + Strategic Direction + CommProtocol + harness all green; (3) WallClockWatchdog fires correctly (`monotonic=309s wall=531s effective=531s >= max_wall_seconds=480s`) → graceful shutdown sequence (30s grace → SIGTERM → 30s deadline → `os._exit(75)`) → atexit fallback writes partial summary.json; (4) Master-flag-FALSE-equivalent behavior holds (`JARVIS_L2_BRANCHING_STRATEGY=bfs` does not perturb non-L2 paths); (5) 6 background ops completed normally during steady-state. **What the soak did NOT exercise** (honest functionality gap): the strategy gate at `RepairEngine.run()` engages ONLY when an op reaches L2 repair, and L2 fires ONLY when VALIDATE exhausts. None of the 12 background ops dispatched (`backlog`/`runtime_health`/`cadence_synthetic`/`doc_staleness` triggers) generated candidates that failed VALIDATE — so `_maybe_run_treefinement` was never called, `register_production_factory_at_boot` never fired, no branches were created, no `.jarvis/ouroboros/repair_tree.jsonl` rows written. This is the byte-identical rollback contract working AS DESIGNED — the gate stays inert when L2 doesn't fire. **The functionality validation gap requires deliberately L2-triggering ops**: real-world bug-fix ops in production (operator-paced; arrives naturally over time), OR a future `JARVIS_L2_FORCE_REPAIR_FAILURE_RATE` synthetic-failure-injection knob (engineering arc), OR — most pragmatically — **SWE-Bench-Pro evaluation** (each benchmark problem ships with failing tests, so every problem naturally triggers L2 → tree mode → full production wiring exercised under realistic load). SWE-Bench-Pro is therefore BOTH an external benchmark AND the natural tree-mode exercise harness. **Soak findings document the honest split**: wiring SAFETY validated end-to-end; tree-mode FUNCTIONALITY requires an exercise harness that the existing background-op infrastructure does not provide. **Next step**: SWE-Bench-Pro arc (planned in v3.4 §40.7.7-op as the next §40.7-citation follow-on; ~2-3 sessions of focused engineering for harness binding + real evaluation runtime). Per-arc full provenance: `memory/project_v3_5_treefinement_first_validation_soak.md`. Prior version note retained:

— v3.4 (2026-05-12 — **Treefinement L2 OPERATIONAL — production wiring closes the v3.3 deferred gap**: The strategy gate shipped in v3.3 was structurally REACHABLE but BEHAVIORALLY a no-op (no production factory registered). The v3.4 six-phase production-wiring arc (A→F) ships the canonical factory + adapter + lazy boot wiring end-to-end. **Phase A** extracts `RepairEngine._generate_repair_candidate` from the inline GENERATE block in `_run_inner` as the single-source provider invocation primitive; `_run_inner` sha256 bytes-pin atomically re-locked at `9e881fdde25ec5b1` (LINEAR semantics byte-equivalent; verified by 10/10 existing `test_repair_engine` tests staying green). **Phase B** ships `GitApplyDiffApplier` (production `DiffApplier` Protocol impl) using the safe `asyncio.create_subprocess_exec` API (program + args list — no shell, no command-injection surface) wrapping the canonical `git apply --whitespace=nowarn`; 5-stage discipline (validate → parse → capture-old → apply → capture-new); 8 structured error codes (`empty_diff` / `no_targets_in_diff` / `read_old_failed` / `git_not_installed` / `git_subprocess_failed` / `git_apply_timeout` / `git_apply_failed:exit<N>` / `read_new_failed`). **Phase C** ships `ProductionBranchGenerator` (production `BranchGenerator` Protocol impl) composing Phase A primitive + Phase 3 `maybe_inject_sibling_outcomes` (cross-branch substrate) + canonical `RepairContext` shape via `_AugmentedRepairContext` wrapper with additive `cross_branch_outcomes` field; provider's existing prompt-construction code reads canonical fields transparently while future provider extensions may consume the new field. **Phase D** ships `production_tree_runner_factory` (zero-arg `Callable[[], Awaitable[RepairTreeResult]]` invocation closure — single-call invariant) composing 7 canonical surfaces (WorktreeManager + GitApplyDiffApplier + TestRunner + SemanticGuardian + CanonicalBranchValidator + ProductionBranchGenerator + RepairTreeRunner); pure-function `tree_result_to_repair_result` deterministic adapter over closed `LayerVerdict × BranchOutcome` taxonomies (WON_TERMINAL → L2_CONVERGED with diff + file_path extracted via Phase B's `extract_diff_targets`; EXHAUSTED → `treefinement_exhausted`; BUDGET_TERMINAL → `treefinement_budget_terminal`; empty → `treefinement_empty_result`; unexpected verdict → `treefinement_unexpected_verdict:<value>`; adapter exception → `treefinement_adapter_failed:<exc>`); Phase 5 stub `_invoke_tree_factory` replaced with 3-stage pipeline (construct closure → await tree result → adapt to RepairResult) where ANY stage failure returns None (gate falls through to LINEAR byte-identically); only `asyncio.CancelledError` propagates. **Phase E** ships `register_production_factory_at_boot` lazy registration on first `_maybe_run_treefinement` call (idempotent: second/third calls no-op; operator-override-respecting: never overwrites a custom factory; ## §40 ADVANCED FORWARD ROADMAP (post-tonight, operator-paced)

Per Explore agent survey of docs/architecture/ + memory/ + CLAUDE.md manifesto + PHD_STRATEGIC_PATH.md, the forward items are organized into **3 tiers by RSI-leverage**, not engineering scope.

### §40.1 Tier 1 — Recursion-bounding (load-bearing for second-order doll)

These directly enable safe recursive self-modification. **Each is structurally required before O+V can safely modify its own governance**:

1. **RRD §1 Boundary recursion-depth gate** (~2-3d) — Per Explore agent finding #2 + PHD_STRATEGIC_PATH.md §4: when M10 ArchitectureProposer can propose changes to `backend/core/ouroboros/governance/` itself, infinite regress is possible. Add deterministic gate (post-PLAN, mirroring Iron Gate exploration-first) that forbids proposals from modifying governance without operator approval. Composes existing TerminationHookRegistry + IronGate patterns.

2. **Hash-cap on self-modification (cryptographic signature gate)** — Every commit touching `backend/core/ouroboros/governance/` carries operator's last-approved AST checksum. If system modifies governance, signature breaks → AutoCommitter refuses to land. Composes existing change_engine + AutoCommitter signature path.

3. **Antivenom self-immunization** (~1w) — When SemanticGuardian flags a pattern, generate K mutations of that exact pattern and re-test. If guardian can't catch the mutations, auto-file a hardening op against itself. Composes existing semantic_guardian.py master kill switch + per-pattern toggles.

4. **M10 ArchitectureProposer graduation contract** (~2-3h) — Per Explore agent finding #1: M10 substrate is 70% complete (UnhandledPatternMiner, ProposalSynthesizer, 5-layer validation all shipped). Slice 5 graduation contract never wired. Closing this completes the weak-form ontogeny loop: detection → proposal → empirical validation → integration.

### §40.2 Tier 2 — Antivenom completeness + cross-session coherence

5. **SemanticGuardian ↔ MCP boundary** (~1-2w) — Per Explore agent finding #3 + CLAUDE.md §90: SemanticGuardian's 11 injection detectors tune for internal tools. External MCP tools (GitHub MCP, Drive MCP) aren't pattern-matched. Add MCP server whitelist + pattern-delta detection + post-tool-call output scanning for injection signatures. Closes the "first-class MCP" claim.

6. **Vector #5 cross-session coherence harness** (~1-2w) — Per Explore agent finding #4: Move 7 + Move 4 + M9 measure drift mathematically. The system hasn't run long enough (>7 days continuous, >50 ops) to validate repeated runs converge (signatures stabilize, lessons persist). Build empirical closure-verdict rig that reads final session summaries + plots coherence curves. Feeds PhD §6 dissertation eval.

7. **Counterfactual rehearsal mode** (~2-3d) — Run proposed risky changes against last N sessions' op states as counterfactual replay corpus BEFORE applying. CC literally cannot do this (no session memory). O+V has CausalityDAG + session_archive — wire them. Closes a structural moat over CC.

8. **Adversarial autobiography** (~2d) — Run `/adversarial generate` on recent commits to find inputs that would have broken them. Catches Quine-shaped hallucinations that already shipped. Composes Phase 9.4 corpus + AutoCommitter. Closes Vector #7 empirically (only currently-🟠 vector).

### §40.3 Tier 3 — Calibration, learning, second-order metrics

9. **Belief revision ledger** (~3d) — Every PostmortemEngine assertion gets structured claim + falsifying-evidence hooks. When evidence contradicts, file revision op + SemanticGuardian weighs that domain lower. Bayesian calibration learning.

10. **Sleep consolidation pass** (~1.5d) — Idle >30 min → REM-equivalent: replay recent ops fast-forward against DreamEngine blueprints, auto-graduate blueprints that NOW match real patterns. Biological-sleep analog.

11. **Postmortem fusion** (~2d) — After K postmortems mention same root cause, synthesize meta-postmortem proposing structural fix. Learning across failures at architectural scale.

12. **Schelling-point consensus prior** (~3d) — Add deterministic high-confidence baseline prior to Move 6.5 K-roll dispatch. If majority of rolls beat Schelling point, accept; otherwise fall back. Calibrates whether priors found better approaches or just shuffled.

13. **Anti-fragility budget per-module** (~4d) — Track which ops produce reliable outcomes vs flaky ones per-module. Low-budget modules get more validation cycles. Calibrates trust empirically.

14. **Mirror-self test** (~3d) — System periodically reproduces own canonical behavior from CLAUDE.md spec. If implementation drifts from spec, file repair ops. The system tests itself against its own documentation.

15. **Second-order doll completion metric** (~3h) — `metrics/second_order_doll_completed.py` watches for commit signature: `feat()` touching `backend/core/ouroboros/governance/` AND `AutoCommitter` produced it AND it passed all gates. Cheapest path to measuring whether RSI is actually accelerating.

16. **Compositional curiosity** (~1d) — SemanticIndex detects when two clusters have grown without cross-pollination (no commits touching both clusters' modules) — connective-tissue gap. Auto-propose integration op. Composes existing semantic_index.clusters.

17. **ConversationBridge V1.2 voice integration** (~3-5d) — Per Explore agent finding #6 + CLAUDE.md §142: v1.2 backlog explicitly lists "wire `record_turn(source='voice')` from `backend/voice/`". Authority-free by design (only feeds StrategicDirection). Closes the Communicator context feedback loop.

### §40.4 Truly experimental (research-grade, deferred)

18. **Predictive postmortem** (~1w) — Before APPLY, system predicts what postmortem would say if op succeeds vs fails. Reconcile post-VERIFY. Forces calibration.

19. **Proof carrier transport** — Generated fixes produce a proof artifact (formal or test-shaped) that travels with the patch. Future ops in same area respect the invariant. Carrying invariants forward structurally.

20. **Cross-repo causal mirror** (trigger-gated on J-Prime/Reactor-Core arrival, ~2w) — Commits in JARVIS that might affect J-Prime's contracts auto-emit cross_repo_ripple SSE event. Repos talk via predictions, not requests.

21. **Cognitive load shedding** — When SemanticIndex centroid drifts >X over Y days, system refuses new exploration until consolidation cycles bring it back. Bounded curiosity → bounded RSI scope.

22. **Meta-prior learning** (Move 6.5 follow-on, ~1w) — After 100+ multi-prior observations, learn which style_hint priors dominate which task complexity classes. Operator-tuned via observation, not hand-curated. Composes Slice 6 graduation contract.

### §40.5 Chronological prioritization — all 22 items ranked by impact + sequencing

**How to read this table**: items are listed in **execution order** (not item-number order), grouped into 4 chronological waves. Each wave's items have **no inter-wave dependencies** — they can ship in any order within their wave. Cross-wave dependencies are noted in the **Depends-on** column. The **Impact** column rates each item's contribution to A+ grade (HIGH = closes a 🟡 / 🟠 vector OR adds a capability CC structurally cannot have; MEDIUM = compounds existing capability; LOW = refinement / experimental).

**Wave 1 — Foundation telemetry (week 1, ~3-5 days total)**: cheap RSI-acceleration probes that produce data the later waves need.

| Exec order | Item # | Title | Effort | Impact | Depends-on | Rationale |
|-----------|--------|-------|--------|--------|------------|-----------|
| 1 | 15 | Second-order doll completion metric | ~3h | **HIGH** | none | Cheapest path to *measuring* whether RSI is accelerating. Watches for specific commit signature (`feat()` touching governance/ + AutoCommitter produced + all gates passed). Without this metric, Waves 2-4 ship blind. |
| 2 | 4 | M10 ArchitectureProposer graduation contract | ~2-3h | **HIGH** | none | Closes weak-form ontogeny loop: detection → proposal → empirical validation → integration. Substrate 70% complete; just needs graduation contract wired. |
| 3 | 8 | Adversarial autobiography | ~2d | **HIGH** | #15 (uses doll metric to know when to fire) | Closes only remaining 🟠 vector (#7 Quine-shape cage bypass) empirically. Composes Phase 9.4 corpus + AutoCommitter. |
| 4 | 16 | Compositional curiosity (two-clusters-meet) | ~1d | **MEDIUM** | none | Detects connective-tissue gaps via SemanticIndex cluster cross-pollination analysis. Auto-proposes integration ops. |

**Wave 2 — Recursion bounding (week 2-3, ~7-10 days total)**: load-bearing safety for second-order doll. **Each is structurally required before O+V can safely modify its own governance**.

| Exec order | Item # | Title | Effort | Impact | Depends-on | Rationale |
|-----------|--------|-------|--------|--------|------------|-----------|

### §40.5.1 Top-3 if you want to start TODAY

If energy is finite, **start here** — these are the 3 items with maximum impact-per-effort + lowest dependency burden:

1. **#15 Second-order doll completion metric** (~3h) — cheapest RSI-acceleration probe; produces data Waves 2-4 need
2. **#4 M10 ArchitectureProposer graduation contract** (~2-3h) — closes weak-form ontogeny loop; substrate 70% already there
3. **#8 Adversarial autobiography** (~2d) — closes the only remaining 🟠 vector (#7 Quine-shape cage bypass) empirically

These three combined: **~3-5 days of focused work**. Each completes a measurable closure. Together they unlock Waves 2-4 with hard data to drive prioritization.

### §40.5.2 Anti-recommendation

**Do NOT build operator-facing curiosity proposal feed** (rejected from list). Making operator the preference oracle reduces autonomy — save for future supervised-mode if non-architect users ever onboard. This is a Tier-0 (reactive CC-style) pattern that contradicts O+V's autonomy mandate.

The cage was then hardened against all three **static-fixable evasion classes** — synonym-constructs (95f #69280), indirection/aliasing (95g #69281), constant-propagation (95h #69282) — **zero clean-control false positives**, an adversarial-review-caught fail-open FP fixed pre-merge. Residual = eval/deserialize of runtime-constructed values = the §43 Arc 5 OS-containment boundary. **Open:** the empirical post-hardening descent re-measurement is gated on Anthropic credits (the interception is unit-proven).
